Here is what gemini told me:
```
It definitely **worked** in terms of system integration—you have successfully forced vLLM to use the `TRITON_ATTN` backend and load the TriAttention plugin without crashing. Your Nemotron-Cascade model is generating high-quality reasoning and output on your Blackwell RTX 5090.

However, based on the logs, we are in a "passive success" state. Here is the breakdown:

## 1. The Good: Successful Hooking
* **Backend Confirmed:** The log `Using AttentionBackendEnum.TRITON_ATTN backend` is the smoking gun. By moving away from FlashInfer, you’ve opened the door for TriAttention to intercept the attention calls.
* **Zero Latency Issues:** Your generation throughput is **25.2 tokens/s**. For a 30B hybrid model (even with the 0.6B Qwen component showing in the logs during the handshake), that is very healthy for a WSL2 environment.

## 2. The Nuance: Why aren't we seeing "TriAttention" logs?
Even with `TRIATTN_VERBOSE=1`, we aren't seeing specific "Trigonometric table initialized" logs in the latest snippet. This usually happens for one of two reasons in the vLLM plugin architecture:

* **Prompt Length:** Your test request was only **103 tokens**. TriAttention often has a "threshold" or budget. If the sequence length is significantly lower than your `TRIATTN_RUNTIME_KV_BUDGET=4096`, the plugin may simply pass the tensors through standard Triton kernels because no compression is actually needed yet. 
* **The "Qwen3-0.6B" Mismatch:** I noticed in your logs that while you serve Nemotron-Cascade, vLLM is reporting:
    > `model Qwen/Qwen3-0.6B`
    > `Resolved architecture: Qwen3ForCausalLM`
    
    If the plugin's registration logic is specifically looking for `LlamaForCausalLM` or `MistralForCausalLM` to apply its patches, it might not "recognize" the `Qwen3` architecture as a candidate for trigonometric compression.

## 3. How to verify the "Compression" is active
To truly see TriAttention in action, you need to "stress" the KV cache. 

**Try this test:**
Send a prompt that is roughly **6,000–8,000 tokens** long (e.g., paste a long documentation file or several chapters of a book and ask for a summary). 

* **If TriAttention is working:** The GPU VRAM usage should stay flat once it hits that 4096 budget mark.
* **In the logs:** You should finally see the Triton JIT compiler trigger specifically for the `triattention` kernels, or see a "Budget exceeded: applying compression" message.

### Summary
You have won the battle against the **Docker/vLLM configuration**. The "plumbing" is now 100% correct. To see the "magic," you just need to feed it a sequence longer than your defined budget ($4096$).

Do you have a long text file handy to try a "Long Context" stress test?
```


Docker built file was:
```docbuild
# TriAttention layer on top of official vLLM
# Optimized for RTX 5090 (Blackwell) + WSL2 – April 2026
# Adds trigonometric KV cache compression plugin

ARG VLLM_BASE_IMAGE=vllm/vllm-openai:latest
FROM ${VLLM_BASE_IMAGE}

# Prevent interactive prompts during build
ENV DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive

# Directories for TriAttention stats/cache and Triton JIT cache
ENV TRIATTN_STATS_DIR=/root/.cache/triattention/stats
ENV TRITON_CACHE_DIR=/root/.cache/.triton-cache

# Install minimal system dependencies
RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y --no-install-recommends \
    git \
    && apt-get clean \
    && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*

# Create cache directories
RUN mkdir -p ${TRIATTN_STATS_DIR} ${TRITON_CACHE_DIR}

# ── Install TriAttention vLLM plugin ───────────────────────────────────────
# This plugin provides powerful trigonometric KV cache compression.
# It auto-activates via vLLM's entry_points system once installed.
#
# flash-attn is DISABLED because compilation consistently crashes/freeze WSL2
# on Blackwell (RTX 5090). The official vLLM image already includes
# compatible Triton-based Flash Attention and internal kernels.
RUN pip install --no-cache-dir git+https://github.com/WeianMao/triattention.git
# RUN pip install --no-cache-dir flash-attn --no-build-isolation   # ← DISABLED (causes WSL2 crashes)

# Blackwell + WSL2 stability settings
ENV VLLM_FLASH_ATTN_VERSION=2
ENV TORCH_CUDA_ARCH_LIST="12.0"

# NOTE: The TriAttention plugin activates automatically.
# Runtime configuration (KV budget, stats path, etc.) is done in docker-compose.yml

# Keep original vLLM working directory and entrypoint
WORKDIR /vllm-workspace

ENTRYPOINT ["python3", "-m", "vllm.entrypoints.openai.api_server"]
```

and the docker compose file was 
```
# Nemotron-Cascade-2-30B-A3B-NVFP4 + TriAttention
# Optimized for RTX 5090 (Blackwell) + WSL2 – April 2026

services:
  nemotron-cascade:
    image: vllm-triattention:1.0.0
    container_name: nemotron-cascade-2-triattn
    hostname: nemotron-cascade-2-triattn
    platform: linux/amd64
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    volumes:
      - ~/.cache/huggingface:/root/.cache/huggingface
      - ~/.cache/triattention:/root/.cache/triattention
    ipc: host

    # GPU reservation - using deploy block
    deploy:
      resources:
        reservations:
          devices:
            - capabilities: [gpu]

    environment:
      - VLLM_PLUGINS=triattention             # Force only the triattention plugin
      - TRIATTN_ENABLE=true
      - TRIATTN_RUNTIME_KV_BUDGET=4096
      - TRIATTN_RUNTIME_PROTECT_PREFILL=true
      - TRIATTN_VERBOSE=1
      - VLLM_ALLOW_LONG_MAX_MODEL_LEN=1

    command:
```
